de l’estopement de la verge	regarding the stopping of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu. Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout .i. spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme: puis met ou pertus .i. clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi .iij. jors ou iiij. et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	No child is born without testicles, or if they are small, or not in their proper position. If it happens immediately that there should pierce completely all .i. very subtle spatumile according to this form: then place or let the testicles .i. delicate clo of tin, and tie and keep like this for .ij. days or iiij.,and when they want to urinate, remove the clo, and urinate, and then put it back; and by chance no point applies, because the urine that comes out does not allow it to be closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera. Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie. puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de .ij. pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Fold the shoulder bones together and bind them in two layers so that none of the joints through which they pass can allow an abscess to enter or spread;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc .ij. dois de celui, et aprés ces .ij. liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	Apply the bandage along with the first long line, about two spans of that length, and after these two lines leave a little slack equal to the thickness of one span at the back of your knee where there's no space for pus to spread.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	And after that follow the roundness of what he has placed; then cut in the area near the skin of your knee until you can't reach the bone and ligament as we have said earlier.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	Then apply wet wool in oil, and place it on the wounds, and put on the bandage as we have said.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And not once is the white scab burned that we have said, after incision, by fear of blood loss.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	For this happens many times, and let the wound bleed from itself until it stops; and if it doesn't fall off on its own, then apply hot water, and place what we have said there until it stops bleeding.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then continue to treat the wound with another method, until it heals completely.
de hernie carnouse	of fatty hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this part of the treatise, I never see anyone who dare to perform surgery with a metal tool.

Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil. dou chastrement	of sexual restraint
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. de erratique	Regarding the irregularity
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. des emorroides	Of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation. Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that often lack proper care, and when hemorrhoids are old they become painful; we have already discussed their appearances, signs, and I will now describe those that require treatment. Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment. Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	Craft is first among the skills to know how natural birth looks when it occurs, and you'll recognize these signs when you see a woman's water break, and she begins to desire to push out with her breath: at that point, the infant will quickly make an attempt to emerge; then you can tell this birth is proceeding naturally, and its course follows the head first, followed by the rest of it; and upon seeing these signs, you should gently press on her abdomen, so that the child emerges promptly; for when he descends through his head, his rest accompanies him, and his delivery is cleansed of excess with a good birthing process; anything other than this does not occur naturally. For it happens only from his feet, and it forces the body or the legs, and hands, or it occurs from his belly, or genitals, and becomes reversed by chance around his neck, and through other ill-fated arrangements; in these matters craft must be wise and subtle, avoiding error and deception, and I will show you all the signs on how they should assist.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	If the child descends through its head in natural birth, and the woman experiences severe pain during labor, and her strength is weak, she should sit on a chair or have women hold her; then rise from her nature with something cooked from fenugreek, and then place the midwife between her hands with a small spatula which has this form:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.Et se les .ij. mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus .i. siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And cut the second part [of the birthing process], and keep to her finger until all moisture inside her is expelled; while keeping her belly pressed throughout as the child descends, if it does not descend then you must administer castor oil to the woman with fenugreek, along with olive oil. Then have her rise slowly and snort deeply several times, hold her mouth and nose for an hour: now this child emerges. Then remove the stool from under her, cut her, ensuring she does not pass any feces during the process; if her hands cannot enter and the child has died, then take her hands with the knife mentioned beforehand and extract the infant, and do so gently.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piez	From the birth of the child upon its feet

de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	From the child's position on its knees.

si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If you don't move it, then one cannot measure it.

S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it's done like this, that's well. If not, there can't be another way to do it.

des emorroydes	of lacerations
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Loses are of two types: or they are within the foundation, like a piece of pine resin, and if there's small ones and large ones, and in that place blood collects,

dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	so that drying occurs due to fire or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is the drying effect of dung in the intestines, and due to the nature's constraint, and when the disease is old and medicine no longer works.

dou fremit	When the tremor
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Antennae are a tiny false appearance before the body, and they move quite far forward;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part. de la forme dou clistere	in the shape of a bladder
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	None of the times does one make an argentary blister or an iron blister, or a lead blister; and none of these small and large instruments are made according to those to whom they are applied.

et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and there should be an opening where the belly is bound, as you see, and the head is pierced inside; and have two points on one side of the body, and on the other side one each;

des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have discussed the treatment of wounds in the previous section; now we will discuss treatments for hands and medicine, according to completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse depending on how they are made, and depending on where the wounds are located, and for what reason they were caused.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	Things that result from wounds are due to the breaking of bone, and the size of a sword or knife cut, or of an arrow or spear or axe, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or those that are made according to the parts of the body, such as a wound on the neck, or on the head, or on the chest, or in the belly, or in the liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and start with wounds of the simple head, since the memory will come to its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes or to the head, and if the bone isn't broken, be careful whether it's due to stone or similar things, and even though the skin is completely torn and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	And you slightly doubt about the abscess: if it becomes so quickly healthy of the cephalic itself even if there is a little blood from the wound, and let it heal in contrast to the part removed;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And beware that the patient becomes full of wine and rich meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to heal quickly, let his food be reduced, and do not give him wine or meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And place it over the wound, if there is an abscess that breaks open, use a wet cotton soaked in rose oil or only vinegar.

et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound has been contaminated, apply some dressings until it is clean.

And if the wound is large, like from a sword cut or similar injuries, and the lips cannot be sewn together with sutures, then they are sewn together, like I will explain in injuries to the abdomen, by sewing.

Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or discover putrefaction, and it extends to the bone, then remove all the putrefaction, and cleanse with water, then treat it;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which cannot be stopped by medicine, then remove the artery, and if you find it protruding, tie it with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not help, then apply the cautery.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light: and you should apply this powder which binds in such a way that once it's applied, the wound heals.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the way of making this powder is as follows: take one part of incense; dragon's blood two parts; powdered live charcoal three parts, and finely ground it,
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply the powder to the wound, then press firmly until it is well aired and joins fully with all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then keep it properly bandaged, letting it alone without removing the medicine as long as it doesn't swell; for the medicine should be kept until the wound heals.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And you should not do this with charcoal alone, when you don't have the incense or the dragon's blood, but only that the doctor has cleansed the wound.

de la plaie dou col	from the wound in the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This wound comes from the neck and if it is simple, there should be no difference between it and those in the head, but if a vein or an artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's the nose, there should be no other tool than to let the treatment proceed and not put any restraining thing on it, for it harms the nose and causes it to recede;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not put anything cold on the wound, for the material of bones is cold, and continuity with them is connected to the brain, which is the highest part of the body.

et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	And other stones within, according to this manner, and wet applications.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, so it binds in layers, then treat until it heals properly.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and filled with blood, then pierce them or as far down as possible;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is severed, and blood starts to flow outwards, then uncover it or as far down as necessary, and if required, sew it up and cauterize.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if it is cut at the throat or the lungs, or where the windpipe goes, by which the flesh flows,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if you sew up the lung above the stalk of the throat, and do not touch the throat but place it according to its natural form;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then allow the wound to heal properly, and leave it for several days, then treat with desiccated ointments until it heals properly;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the injury has made an impression in the bone, then address it;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	And if there are bone fragments, extract them thoroughly if you can, and leave those that you cannot have until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And let it be drained and treated with its discharge;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there are bones in the wound and it has an ulcer, treat it as I have described in this chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	From the wound of a spear or a knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it's from a spear or a knife, and the wound goes deep, then observe whether there is an increase in windiness around the wound: if so, you will know that the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it's not deep and is full of its blood everywhere, if you don't put the powder on or tie it immediately in the first hour after injury, do not let the blood stop flowing completely because of that.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and give him courage and keep him busy;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply the attractive ointment, and bind it twice each day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you do not have an ointment, place old cotton in the wound to absorb moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient rest on the wound for three days, or four, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if there is no spasm, nor bad heart tremblement, nor Alainne's movements;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see the good arrangements, if you know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Therefore treat it with various remedies and other treatments, until it heals;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	And if it cannot heal or improve, then know that there is an abscess; treat it accordingly.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife cut and it's simple, or worse or on the back, then treat according to what is in front of you.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it's large, use stitches; and if it's small, use powder, and if there are impregnations in the bone, and if you have cut out pieces, if clean the wound, and remove any foreign objects if they are exposed;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they aren't exposed, let the wound fester, if it facilitates the removals;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other limbs, is the judgment like what we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	regarding the protrusion of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The belly decompositions are large and medium-sized and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a major wound, sometimes the bowel jumps out, or the nerves of the intestines, by which there is an intrusion of them;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And the suture is more troublesome, and not once is it as bad as a small wound compared to a large one.
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Therefore, when putting the intestines back in, we would not place them directly, but rather little by little;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	Because when their intestines swell up as soon as they feel cold, they return further into the anus,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because of this, they stimulate the abdominal wound, for thus we must move their intestines back to where they normally are, as is done with other cases.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that there are four ways a rupture of the belly occurs:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common stitches happen at the abdominal stitch,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	And the suturing of other wounds from the body, and two other types of suture specific to their own kind, are common for other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And yet, they are more appropriate with the suture of the belly, and I will say each one and explain.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing of the intestine sticks out,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And if the injured area can be repaired, this can be done through one of these two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when he is cold, warm him up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	moisten a sponge or half a pound of cloth only in water,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	when you cook with boiling water streaming and cypress and thorn,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and as long as the herbs swell so they are cut;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and once this vinegar is strained and made to cook until it frees up, it is ready for reducing.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling depart, you should moisten the intestines with water or with broth that has been well cooked.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for because this allows entry to very little thing;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, they will make a small incision with the tool used for removing the worms;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first treatment is to grind that which has been cut,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	that we should not cut without great necessity or cause;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and these are the instruments to split them:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside in the bend and not outside, and here is how it should look:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound has been enlarged, and the intestines have jumped out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	If you set it back according to its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the ability, because this is what it takes to move it.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide and it's located in the abdominal area,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	If it is necessary to make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and place his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it's in the abdominal region,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	then place the head and buttocks higher than the abdominal region,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if there is a rupture in the abdomen in one of the two parts,
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	If you understand this, let the removed part be higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus, it is necessary to apply what I say in large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use what suits you,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have among your hands .i., a minister who heals the entire wound with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	And gather the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of stitches,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you should take one needle or more, according to the size of the wound's width,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	Then leave about half an inch from the edge of the wound and insert one needle with about an inch of strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierces both leather cheeks with both needle of the spathula,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is inside the leather from within, until you make it pierce that part.
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and join both ends of the needle of the spathula with four units;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then pull through a doubled thread into one part of the needle twice,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then gather together both sides of the wound's opening,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave one inch of space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then weave the thread in the same way you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and keep doing this according to how you need to work with the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Until all the wound is contained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and are of average size, between delicate and thick needles,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	for delicate needles pierce all the flesh, and the overly large can't enter properly:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	thus they should be of medium size;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not right to push the needles too far out from the flesh and skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	let them not pierce and fester the wound before the stitch;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then remove the heads of the needles, so they do not irritate the patient at night;
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and place tents or cloths over the heads of the needles to keep them in position;
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and let them grow until the wound has healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of sewing with needles is more convenient for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it requires only one needle.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second type of stitching is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And you should join the two shoulder joints with skin and the two elbow joints together on one needle where there is a strong thread in half;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced these joints all four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then remove the needle from the part where you started, in the way one sews with thread;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and leave a space between each stitch as wide as a small coin;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this sewing stitch makes the body,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew a wound where there was once an opening or belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which had been cut by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was more than a palm in size,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and let them be large for the intestines to fit properly.
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	And the wound is within the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I brought back the intestine, and it was twenty-one hours since its removal.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound healed up to fifteen days, I treated it, and it became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And when the sight had judged that he would die, and this was a wonder;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and did not cure him with ointment because I was in the first level where one could not find it, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I changed the cloth under the wound four times a day and washed it with honey water until it was clean.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	And I will tell you the two proper ways of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and at first place it from the outer part down to here inside;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When it has pierced straight through the artery in the right way, if you find the head of the syringe or causes pain or where you have inserted the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and make it pierce from the inner part to here on the outside;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	And as for this stitch, know that you must sew them in the same way as the weaver sews his cloth,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And when you leave out the stitch on one side, and take it again from another, until the seam is entirely completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of sewing up, as Galen properly stated,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	So it is like what everyone does, assembling the two parts naturally together,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one end of the thread to the other end in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	Prick with a needle or pierce near the navel, and puncture just that spot.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and leave those two joints at the side;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle, and puncture it from below up to this inside.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	like those two joints on the side;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both on the outer part up to that inside, in two other shoulder joints which are opposite each other;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the common way of stitching and the most usual method.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	The doctors say this word, and none testify to it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One must stitch the abdomen with two needles, or where there is thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	And one must push a needle from one side, and the other from another, like those who sew wounds;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	Know that when the rupture is in the midst of the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	The suture there is more painful than in any other part of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is as follows: (This refers to assessing and treating wounds similar to others.)
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	And it is that when you find the wound fresh with all its blood, as long as the surgeon has moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	so that he may be placed with his intestines back inside, and the stitches; then put on a powder to soothe the wound,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if the surgeon has moved them, apply no ointment that might be present, until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	And heat the thread, and may they sew up the cut, and mend it;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound in the same way as others, until it is cleaned;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you do not have medicines, put an old cotton cloth, temporarily, when it starts to weep.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And shake it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you need no other medicine besides in many situations when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound might cause communication with principal parts of the body,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	then it is necessary for you to immerse a thread lightly in oil heated by fire, or in rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it inside the joints, and under the skin;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	And if one feels pain or gangrene in the bowels, and this occurs frequently.
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	If black wine enemas are given, and equally if gangrene reaches up to the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And penetrates within, and remember that when it's in the large intestine, it is easier to heal than in the smaller ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestines which are called "juvenile" cannot be healed when they are injured,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And this is due to the arrangement of veins that they are, and by the subtlety of all the body, and the approach of its nature to the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the heart jumps out of the wound, then place it back inside as with an intestine, while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it is old and has become red or black, then you must tie the area that is black, so that no further blood comes out,
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	because there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then take what is between the link,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place both shoulders up to beyond the wound until they ease the extraction when the joints are cold, and let the wound heal.
de la routure dou boueil	from the rupture of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are full, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	if it can be restored in some places,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen that some were pierced or wounded in the stomach by a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And if it became inflamed and turned into a fistula, and there was discharge and wind flowing out of it;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied treatment according to what I could do, and did not stop refining until it was healed, and sealed the wounds.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it healed, I wondered if the patient might have pain in their belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	There was no harm, but they remained in better condition, eating and drinking.
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And they say that when there is a small wound inside the intestine, it must be treated like this:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take large pieces of fat, then join together the edges of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the fat has opened its mouth, place it on the two edges,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if its mouth joins together;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then he grasps the head, and this is held so that it cannot be released,
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then makes another vibration in this manner as before, until the wound is completely treated;
et cout la plaie.	and finishes the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	Those who are so inflamed in the intestines, and do not cause any harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	And if one could tie the intestine with a fine thread which has been cut from an animal's intestine,
en teil maniere:	in a similar manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the head of this intestines thread so that it comes out chewed,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie its head to this thread with a single strand of fine linen string.
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then thread the needle with the string, stitch the intestine together, and realign it at the opening;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this method of stitch sewing does nothing other than following the way of practice and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and broad, especially when it's in one of the intestinal cavities, if there's no obstruction or damage, rely on skillfulness.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	from a fistula, or wherever it may be.
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, when it matures, is universally called "fistula",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And similarly when it is covered and begins to heal.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	Fistula refers to a hard and yellowish swelling that is felt without pain, or where there is no sensation of pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And it is covered like the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And sometimes it leaps clearly, and at other times thickly;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Sometimes barely a trickle, and at other times enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have spoken about the classification of wounds, that any unhealed wound, and if there is no pus,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	this can only be due to one of the eight reasons:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	This is to know by the smallness of the blood or the wound;

Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	So it is necessary for me to tell you about the treatment of a fistula which is done through manual work.

dou feu	with fire

Des vils	Of low quality

De la dolor qui vient de ventositeit	Of the pain that comes from wind or cold.
